# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="c85ac-103">Catene di crittografia Microsoft 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c85ac-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c85ac-104">Microsoft 365 utilizza una serie di provider di certificati diversi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c85ac-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c85ac-105">Di seguito viene descritto l'elenco completo dei certificati radice noti di Microsoft 365 che i clienti possono incontrare quando si accede a Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c85ac-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c85ac-106">Per informazioni sui certificati che potrebbe essere necessario installare nella propria infrastruttura, vedere [Plan for Third-Party SSL Certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c85ac-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoft-365/enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c85ac-107">Le informazioni relative al certificato seguenti si applicano a tutte le istanze di Microsoft 365 a livello mondiale e cloud nazionale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c85ac-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>
